                    RoundingFactor::None:

                    RoundingFactor::"1000":
                      RoundingText := Text012;
                    RoundingFactor::"1000000":
                      RoundingText := Text013;
                  END;
                END;

    PreviewMode=PrintLayout;

  CODE
  {
    VAR
      GLSetup@1100529615 : Record 98;
      TmpPrognosisDates@1100529602 : TEMPORARY Record 2000000007;
      TmpPrognosisChartData@1100529604 : TEMPORARY Record 11020579;
      CostGroupPlot@1100529605 : Record 11126038;
      CostGroupGeneralJournal@1100527700 : Record 11126038;
      CostControlMgt@1100529611 : Codeunit 11012006;
      PrognosisMgt@1100529614 : Codeunit 11020217;
      PrognosisDate@1100529601 : Date;
      FilterDate@1100529600 : Date;
      ProjectNo@1100529612 : Code[20];
      ContractAmounts@1100529606 : ARRAY [5] OF Decimal;
      BudgetAmounts@1100529607 : ARRAY [5] OF Decimal;
      InvoiceAmounts@1100529608 : ARRAY [6] OF Decimal;
      PrognosisEndResult@1100529609 : ARRAY [8] OF Decimal;
      WIPAmounts@1100529610 : ARRAY [7] OF Decimal;
      PrognosesCount@1100529603 : Integer;
      MaxPrognosesCount@1100529613 : Integer;
      StartPageNo@1100527701 : Integer;
      RoundingFactor@1100529618 : 'None,1,1000,1000000';
      RoundingText@1100529617 : Text[80];
      NormalFormatString@1100529616 : Text[80];
      Text008@1100529624 : TextConst 'ENU=<Precision,;NOR=<Precision,;SVE=<Precision,';
      Text009@1100529623 : TextConst 'ENU=><Standard Format,0>;NOR=><Standard Format,0>;SVE=><Standard Format,0>';
      Text010@1100529622 : TextConst 'ENU=<Precision,1><Standard Format,0>;NOR=<Precision,1><Standard Format,0>;SVE=<Precision,1><Standard Format,0>';
      Text011@1100529621 : TextConst 'ENU=Amounts are rounded to 1;NOR=Belõp er rundet av til 1;SVE=Belopp avrundas till 1';
      Text012@1100529620 : TextConst 'ENU=Amounts are in whole 1000s.;NOR=Belõpene er i hele 1000.;SVE=Belopp Ñr i hela 1000-tal.';
      Text013@1100529619 : TextConst 'ENU=Amounts are in whole 1000000s.;NOR=Belõpene er i hele 1000000.;SVE=Belopp Ñr i hela 1000000-tal.';

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100529607() : Text;
    VAR
      ProjectFilter0@1100529601 : Text;
      ProjectFilter2@1100529600 : Text;
    BEGIN
      ProjectFilter0 := Project.GETFILTERS;
      Project.FILTERGROUP(2);
      ProjectFilter2 := Project.GETFILTERS;
      Project.FILTERGROUP(0);

      IF (ProjectFilter0 = '') AND (ProjectFilter2 = '') THEN
        EXIT;

      IF ProjectFilter2 <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2, %3', Project.TABLECAPTION, ProjectFilter0, ProjectFilter2))
      ELSE
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', Project.TABLECAPTION, ProjectFilter0));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetPrognosisDate@1100529602();
    VAR
      PrognosisLoc@1100529600 : Record 11012034;
    BEGIN
      PrognosisDate := FilterDate;
      TmpPrognosisDates.DELETEALL;
      PrognosesCount := 0;

      PrognosisLoc.SETRANGE("Project No.", Project."No.");
      PrognosisLoc.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", 0D, FilterDate);
      PrognosisLoc.SETRANGE("Select For Reporting", TRUE);
      IF PrognosisLoc.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT;

      PrognosisLoc.FINDLAST;
      PrognosisDate := PrognosisLoc."Prognosis Date";
      REPEAT
        TmpPrognosisDates."Period Start" := PrognosisLoc."Prognosis Date";
        TmpPrognosisDates.INSERT;
        PrognosesCount += 1;
      UNTIL (PrognosisLoc.NEXT(-1) = 0) OR (PrognosesCount = MaxPrognosesCount);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetPrognosisChartData@1100529600();
    VAR
      ProjectLoc@1100529600 : Record 11072003;
      i@1100529601 : Integer;
      DivBy@1100529602 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TmpPrognosisChartData.DELETEALL;
      IF PrognosesCount = 0 THEN
        EXIT;

      ProjectLoc.GET(Project."No.");
      ProjectLoc.SETRANGE("Project Filter", Project."No.");

      CASE RoundingFactor OF
        RoundingFactor::None,
        RoundingFactor::"1":
          DivBy := 1;
        RoundingFactor::"1000":
          DivBy := 1000;
        RoundingFactor::"1000000":
          DivBy := 1000000;
      END;

      i := PrognosesCount;
      TmpPrognosisDates.FINDSET;
      REPEAT
        TmpPrognosisChartData.INIT;
        TmpPrognosisChartData."Key Code1" := FORMAT(i);
        TmpPrognosisChartData.Date1 := TmpPrognosisDates."Period Start";
        ProjectLoc.SETFILTER("Cumulation Filter", '..%1', TmpPrognosisChartData.Date1);
        ProjectLoc.CALCFIELDS("Actual Costs", Revenues);
        TmpPrognosisChartData.Dec1 := ProjectLoc."Actual Costs" / DivBy;
        TmpPrognosisChartData.Dec2 := ProjectLoc.Revenues / DivBy;

        TmpPrognosisChartData.INSERT;
        i -= 1;
      UNTIL TmpPrognosisDates.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetContractAmounts@1100529605();
    VAR
      ExtensionContract@1100529601 : Record 11012004;
      ProjectPrincipal@1100529602 : Record 11012005;
      i@1100529600 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(ContractAmounts);

      Project.CALCFIELDS("Contract Amount", "Options Contract Amount");
      ContractAmounts[1] := Project."Contract Amount";
      ContractAmounts[3] := Project."Options Contract Amount";

      ExtensionContract.SETRANGE("Main Project No.", Project."Main Project");
      ExtensionContract.SETRANGE("Project No.", Project."No.");
      ExtensionContract.SETFILTER("Version Date", '..%1', PrognosisDate);
      ExtensionContract.SETFILTER(Status, '%1|%2', ExtensionContract.Status::Order, ExtensionContract.Status::"Invoicing Allowed");
      ExtensionContract.CALCSUMS("Contract Amount (LCY)");
      ContractAmounts[2] := ExtensionContract."Contract Amount (LCY)";

      ProjectPrincipal.SETRANGE("Project No.", Project."No.");
      ProjectPrincipal.CALCSUMS("Plot Price");
      ContractAmounts[4] := ProjectPrincipal."Plot Price";

      FOR i := 1 TO 4 DO
        ContractAmounts[5] += ContractAmounts[i];
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetBudgetAmounts@1100529603();
    VAR
      i@1100529600 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(BudgetAmounts);
      PrognosisMgt.CalcTotalPrognosisAmount(Project."No.", PrognosisDate,
        0, '', BudgetAmounts[1], BudgetAmounts[2], BudgetAmounts[3], BudgetAmounts[4]);
      BudgetAmounts[1] += BudgetAmounts[4];
      BudgetAmounts[4] := 0;
      FOR i := 1 TO 4 DO
        BudgetAmounts[5] += BudgetAmounts[i];
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetInvoiceAmounts@1100529604();
    VAR
      ProjectLedgerEntry@1100529600 : Record 11072005;
      CustLedgerEntry@1100529601 : Record 21;
      SalesInvoiceLine@1100529602 : Record 113;
      SalesCrMemoLine@1100529603 : Record 115;
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(InvoiceAmounts);

      ProjectLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Job No.", Project."No.");
      ProjectLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Cost Type", ProjectLedgerEntry."Cost Type"::Revenues);
      ProjectLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date", '..%1', PrognosisDate);
      ProjectLedgerEntry.CALCSUMS("Total Price (LCY)");
      InvoiceAmounts[1] := - ProjectLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)";

      CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Project No.", Project."No.");
      CustLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Document Type", '%1|%2', CustLedgerEntry."Document Type"::Invoice, CustLedgerEntry."Document Type"::"Credit Memo");
      CustLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date", '..%1', PrognosisDate);
      CustLedgerEntry.SETAUTOCALCFIELDS("Original Amt. (LCY)");
      IF CustLedgerEntry.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          InvoiceAmounts[2] += CustLedgerEntry."Original Amt. (LCY)";
        UNTIL CustLedgerEntry.NEXT = 0;

      SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Job No.", Project."No.");
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETFILTER("Posting Date", '..%1', PrognosisDate);
      IF NOT SalesInvoiceLine.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
        CustLedgerEntry.RESET;
        CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Document Type", CustLedgerEntry."Document Type"::Invoice);
        CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE(Open, FALSE);
        CustLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Closed at Date", '..%1', PrognosisDate);

        SalesInvoiceLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.");
        SalesInvoiceLine.FINDSET;
        REPEAT
          SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Document No.", SalesInvoiceLine."Document No.");

          CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Document No.", SalesInvoiceLine."Document No.");
          CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Customer No.", SalesInvoiceLine."Sell-to Customer No.");

          IF CustLedgerEntry.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
            SalesInvoiceLine.CALCSUMS(Amount);
            IF PrognosisDate - SalesInvoiceLine."Posting Date" < 30 THEN
              InvoiceAmounts[3] += SalesInvoiceLine.Amount
            ELSE
              InvoiceAmounts[4] += SalesInvoiceLine.Amount;
          END;

          SalesInvoiceLine.FINDLAST;
          SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Document No.");
        UNTIL SalesInvoiceLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      SalesCrMemoLine.SETRANGE("Job No.", Project."No.");
      SalesCrMemoLine.SETFILTER("Posting Date", '..%1', PrognosisDate);
      IF NOT SalesCrMemoLine.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
        CustLedgerEntry.RESET;
        CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Document Type", CustLedgerEntry."Document Type"::"Credit Memo");
        CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE(Open, FALSE);
        CustLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Closed at Date", '..%1', PrognosisDate);

        SalesCrMemoLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.");
        SalesCrMemoLine.FINDSET;
        REPEAT
          SalesCrMemoLine.SETRANGE("Document No.", SalesCrMemoLine."Document No.");

          CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Document No.", SalesCrMemoLine."Document No.");
          CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Customer No.", SalesCrMemoLine."Sell-to Customer No.");

          IF CustLedgerEntry.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
            SalesCrMemoLine.CALCSUMS(Amount);
            IF PrognosisDate - SalesCrMemoLine."Posting Date" < 30 THEN
              InvoiceAmounts[3] -= SalesCrMemoLine.Amount
            ELSE
              InvoiceAmounts[4] -= SalesCrMemoLine.Amount;
          END;

          SalesCrMemoLine.FINDLAST;
          SalesCrMemoLine.SETRANGE("Document No.");
        UNTIL SalesCrMemoLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      InvoiceAmounts[5] := InvoiceAmounts[3] + InvoiceAmounts[4];
      InvoiceAmounts[6] := ContractAmounts[5] - InvoiceAmounts[1];
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetPrognosisEndResult@1100529606();
    VAR
      PrognosisLine@1100529600 : Record 11012035;
      i@1100529602 : Integer;
      CostType@1100529607 : Option;
      CostObjectFilter@1100529606 : Text;
      EstimateOriginalBudget@1100529605 : Decimal;
      EstimateExtensionBudget@1100529604 : Decimal;
      EstimateOptionsBudget@1100529603 : Decimal;
      EstimateAdjustmentBudget@1100529601 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(PrognosisEndResult);

      PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Project No.", Project."No.");
      PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", PrognosisDate);
      PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Cost Type", PrognosisLine."Cost Type"::Material);
      PrognosisLine.CALCSUMS("Prognosis End Result");
      PrognosisEndResult[1] := PrognosisLine."Prognosis End Result";

      PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Cost Type", PrognosisLine."Cost Type"::Subcontracting);
      PrognosisLine.CALCSUMS("Prognosis End Result");
      PrognosisEndResult[2] := PrognosisLine."Prognosis End Result";

      PrognosisLine.SETFILTER("Cost Type", '<>%1&<>%2', PrognosisLine."Cost Type"::Material, PrognosisLine."Cost Type"::Subcontracting);
      PrognosisLine.CALCSUMS("Prognosis End Result");
      PrognosisEndResult[3] := PrognosisLine."Prognosis End Result";

      PrognosisMgt.CalcEstimateResultPrognosis(Project."No.", PrognosisDate, CostType, CostObjectFilter,
        EstimateOriginalBudget, EstimateExtensionBudget, EstimateOptionsBudget, EstimateAdjustmentBudget);
      IF (CostObjectFilter <> '') AND (EstimateOriginalBudget + EstimateExtensionBudget + EstimateOptionsBudget + EstimateAdjustmentBudget <> 0)
      THEN BEGIN
        PrognosisEndResult[4] := EstimateOriginalBudget + EstimateExtensionBudget + EstimateOptionsBudget + EstimateAdjustmentBudget;
        PrognosisEndResult[3] -= PrognosisEndResult[4];
      END ELSE
        PrognosisEndResult[4] := CostControlMgt.CalcTotalEstimateResult(Project."No.", PrognosisDate);

      FOR i := 1 TO 4 DO
        PrognosisEndResult[5] += PrognosisEndResult[i];

      PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Cost Type");
      PrognosisLine.CALCSUMS("Risc Coverage", "Budget Amount", "Prognosis End Result", "Actual Costs");
      PrognosisEndResult[6] := PrognosisLine."Risc Coverage";
      PrognosisEndResult[7] := PrognosisLine."Budget Amount" - PrognosisLine."Prognosis End Result" - PrognosisLine."Actual Costs";

      IF BudgetAmounts[5] - PrognosisEndResult[4] <> 0 THEN
        PrognosisEndResult[8] := PrognosisEndResult[5] / (BudgetAmounts[5] - PrognosisEndResult[4]);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetWIPAmounts@1100529611();
    VAR
      ProjectLedgerEntry@1100529600 : Record 11072005;
      ProjectInstallment@1100529601 : Record 11012018;
      PrognosisLine@1100529602 : Record 11012035;
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(WIPAmounts);

      PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Project No.", Project."No.");
      PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", PrognosisDate);
      PrognosisLine.CALCSUMS("Actual Costs");
      WIPAmounts[1] := PrognosisLine."Actual Costs";

      ProjectLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Job No.", Project."No.");
      ProjectLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date", '..%1', PrognosisDate);
      ProjectLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Entry Type", ProjectLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::Sale);
      ProjectLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Advance Payment", FALSE);
      IF ProjectLedgerEntry.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        CLEAR(ProjectInstallment);
        REPEAT
          IF ProjectLedgerEntry."Installment No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
            IF (ProjectInstallment."Project No." <> ProjectLedgerEntry."Job No.") OR
               (ProjectInstallment.Principal <> ProjectLedgerEntry.Principal) OR
               (ProjectInstallment."Plot No." <> ProjectLedgerEntry."Plot No.") OR
               (ProjectInstallment."Installment No." <> ProjectLedgerEntry."Installment No.")
            THEN
              ProjectInstallment.GET(ProjectLedgerEntry."Job No.", ProjectLedgerEntry.Principal, ProjectLedgerEntry."Plot No.", ProjectLedgerEntry."Installment No.");

            CASE TRUE OF
              ProjectInstallment."Extension Contract" <> '':
                WIPAmounts[3] -= ProjectLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)";
              ProjectInstallment.Option <> '':
                WIPAmounts[4] -= ProjectLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)";
              ELSE
                IF CostObjBelongsToPlot(ProjectLedgerEntry."Global Dimension 2 Code") THEN
                  WIPAmounts[5] -= ProjectLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)"
                ELSE
                  WIPAmounts[2] -= ProjectLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)";
            END;
          END ELSE
            IF CostObjBelongsToGeneralJournal(ProjectLedgerEntry."Global Dimension 2 Code") THEN
              WIPAmounts[6] -= ProjectLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)";
        UNTIL ProjectLedgerEntry.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      WIPAmounts[7] := WIPAmounts[1] - WIPAmounts[2] - WIPAmounts[3] - WIPAmounts[4] - WIPAmounts[5] - WIPAmounts[6];
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CostObjBelongsToPlot@1100529609(CostObjCode@1100529600 : Code[20]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      CostObjectsByCostGroup@1100529601 : Record 11126039;
    BEGIN
      IF CostGroupPlot.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);

      CostObjectsByCostGroup.SETRANGE("Cost Object Code", CostObjCode);
      IF CostObjectsByCostGroup.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);

      CostGroupPlot.FINDSET;
      REPEAT
        CostObjectsByCostGroup.SETRANGE("Cost Group Code", CostGroupPlot.Code);
        IF NOT CostObjectsByCostGroup.ISEMPTY THEN
          EXIT(TRUE);
      UNTIL CostGroupPlot.NEXT = 0;

      EXIT(FALSE);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CostObjBelongsToGeneralJournal@1100527702(CostObjCode@1100529600 : Code[20]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      CostObjectsByCostGroup@1100529601 : Record 11126039;
    BEGIN
      IF CostGroupGeneralJournal.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);

      CostObjectsByCostGroup.SETRANGE("Cost Object Code", CostObjCode);
      IF CostObjectsByCostGroup.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);

      CostGroupGeneralJournal.FINDSET;
      REPEAT
        CostObjectsByCostGroup.SETRANGE("Cost Group Code", CostGroupGeneralJournal.Code);
        IF NOT CostObjectsByCostGroup.ISEMPTY THEN
          EXIT(TRUE);
      UNTIL CostGroupGeneralJournal.NEXT = 0;

      EXIT(FALSE);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetFilterDate@1100529610();
    VAR
      Prognosis@1100529600 : Record 11012034;
    BEGIN
      IF ProjectNo = '' THEN BEGIN
        FilterDate := 0D;
        EXIT;
      END;

      IF NOT Prognosis.GET(ProjectNo, FilterDate) THEN
        FilterDate := 0D
      ELSE
        IF NOT Prognosis."Select For Reporting" THEN
          FilterDate := 0D;

      IF FilterDate = 0D THEN BEGIN
        Prognosis.SETRANGE("Project No.", ProjectNo);
        Prognosis.SETRANGE("Select For Reporting", TRUE);
        IF Prognosis.FINDLAST THEN
          FilterDate := Prognosis."Prognosis Date";
        EXIT;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE RoundAmount@1100529634(Value@1102 : Decimal) : Text;
    BEGIN
      CASE RoundingFactor OF
        RoundingFactor::None:
          EXIT(FORMAT(Value, 0, NormalFormatString));
        RoundingFactor::"1":
          EXIT(FORMAT((ROUND(Value, 1))));
        RoundingFactor::"1000":
          EXIT(FORMAT(ROUND(Value / 1000, 0.1), 0, Text010));
        RoundingFactor::"1000000":
          EXIT(FORMAT(ROUND(Value / 1000000, 0.1), 0, Text010));
      END;
    END;

    [External]
    PROCEDURE SetCommonParameters@1100529601(NewProjectNo@1100529600 : Code[20];NewFilterDate@1100529601 : Date;NewStartPageNo@1100527701 : Integer;NewRoundingFactor@1100529603 : 'None,1,1000,1000000');
    BEGIN
      ProjectNo := NewProjectNo;
      FilterDate := NewFilterDate;
      StartPageNo := NewStartPageNo;
      RoundingFactor := NewRoundingFactor;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Shared TotalPrinted As Boolean

Public Function LastRowIsTotal(ByVal Value As Boolean) As Boolean
    If TotalPrinted = False Then
        TotalPrinted = Value
        Return False
    End If
    If TotalPrinted = True Then
        TotalPrinted = Value
        Return True
    End If
End Function

Shared Data as Object

Public Function SetData(NewData as Object)
    If NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
        Data = NewData
    End If
End Function

Public Function GetData(Num as Integer) as Object
  Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data),Chr(177))))
End Function
